рдЙрддреНрд╕рд╡рд╛рдГ

рднрджреНрд░рд╛-рдЖрджрд┐-рдкреБрд╖реНрдХрд░-рд╕рдорд╛рдкрдирдореН

Coming from Brahma’s Kamandalu, Pushkara Raja resides in different rivers, along with 3.5 crore tirthas, following the Sankranti of Guru, for twelve days at the beginning of the Sankranti (─Бdi puс╣гkaram) and at the end of the year (preceding transition to the next r─Б┼Ы─л, antya puс╣гkaram), and for two muhurtas during mid-day, every day, during the entire year. Following the transition of Guru to makara r─Б┼Ы─л, puс╣гkarar─Бja resides in bhadr─Б river.

рдХрд╛рдЮреНрдЪреА ремрек рдЬрдЧрджреНрдЧреБрд░реБ рд╢реНрд░реА-рдЪрдиреНрджреНрд░рд╢реЗрдЦрд░реЗрдиреНрджреНрд░ рд╕рд░рд╕реНрд╡рддреА рел рдЖрд░рд╛рдзрдирд╛ #резренреж

Observed on Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зa-Pratham─Б tithi of K─Бrttikaс╕е (lunar) month (Apar─Бhс╣Зaс╕е/vyaapti). The event has been commemorated since it occurred in 4952 (kali era).
Devoted to Lord Chandramauli, preceptor ┼Ъr─л Chandra┼Ыekhara too remaining in the P─лс╣нha for thirtyseven years reached his eternal abode on the first day of Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зapakс╣гa in the month of K─Бrthika of the year S─Бdh─Бraс╣Зa. The name of this preceptor before initiation was Ve├▒katasubrahmaс╣Зya D─лkс╣гita. He was a descendant of the family of Govinda D─лkс╣гita, wellknown as тАЬAyyanтАЭ who carried out many righteous acts of тАЬp┼лrtaтАЭ and adorned the ministerial post in the assembly of King Sevappa N─Бyaka of the N─Бyaka dynasty ruling Thanjavur. This preceptor was well-versed in Mantra ┼Ъ─Бstra. Only during the period of this preceptor, the renovation or reinstallation of the pair of ear-rings (taс╣нaс╣Еka yugala) symbolic of Sricakra, of Goddess Akhil─Бс╣Зde┼Ыvar─л of Jambuke┼Ыvara, renovation of Sricakra in theK─Бm─Бkс╣г─л temple at K─Б├▒ci were carried out. During his visit ot Tanjavur, the preceptor was reverentially coronated with gold or offered Kanak─Бbhiс╣гeka by the monarch who was ruling Tanjavur. ┼Ъalivahana era 1773.

Observed on day 3 of December (gregorian) month. Julian date was converted to Gregorian in this reckoning. The event has been commemorated since it occurred in 1659 (gregorian era).
Day 13 (after Afzal’s death): Supe, Tambe, Pali, Nerle, Kameri, Visapur, Save Uran, Koley are all taken.

Observed on Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зa-Tс╣Ыt─лy─Б tithi of K─Бrttikaс╕е (lunar) month (Apar─Бhс╣Зaс╕е/vyaapti). The event has been commemorated since it occurred in 3170 (kali era).
Kс╣Ыp─Б┼Ыaс╣Еkara, son of ─Аtmasomay─Бji in Andhra in the lineage of Garga, with the name Gaс╣Еgayya before initiation established six religions of worship in worshipping ┼Ъiva, Hari, Skanda and others away from Tantrik practices and establishing everywhere the non-dualism enunciated in the Vedas, drove away the notion of dualism. Kс╣Ыp─Б┼Ыaс╣Еkara established ┼Ъr─л Vi┼Ыvar┼лpa at ┼Ъс╣Ыс╣Еgeri under the directions of ┼Ъr─л Kaivalya Mun─лndra and formulated precepts; having adorned ─Аc─Бrya P─лс╣нha for forty-one years, he departed in the direction of Kubera, viz. North and attained siddhi at Vindhyas. The mighty omniscient (Kс╣Ыp─Б┼Ыaс╣Еkara), the One without a second, attained the supreme non-dual state of the Ultimate known as par─Бpara which is full of Supreme Bliss on the third day of the dark fortnight in the month of K─Бrtika in the year Vibhava.

рдХрд╛рдЮреНрдЪреА резрео рдЬрдЧрджреНрдЧреБрд░реБ рд╢реНрд░реА-рдпреЛрдЧрддрд┐рд▓рдХ рд╕реБрд░реЗрдиреНрджреНрд░ рд╕рд░рд╕реНрд╡рддреА рдЖрд░рд╛рдзрдирд╛ #резремрейрем

Observed on ┼Ъukla-Pratham─Б tithi of M─Бrga┼Ы─лrс╣гaс╕е (lunar) month (Apar─Бhс╣Зaс╕е/vyaapti). The event has been commemorated since it occurred in 3486 (kali era).
The austere preceptor Surendra after defeating boldly in debate the materialist Durdhivi and his companion J─лva, being honoured by King Surendra in his Court merged in his original state. Preceptor Surendra, a Maharashtrian, revered by all as M─Бdhura, resorted to asceticism, an adept in Yogic practices, governed the Maс╣нha for only ten years and reached his abode on the first day of the bright fortnight in the month of M─Бrga┼Ы─лrс╣гa of the T─Бraс╣Зa year in the Kali era 3486.

рдЙрддреНрд╕рд╡рд╛рдГ

рдЧреЛрд╡рд┐рдиреНрдж-рдкрдиреНрдд-рд╣рддреНрдпрд╛ #реиремрез

Observed on day 20 of December (gregorian) month. The event has been commemorated since it occurred in 1760 (gregorian era).
On this day, in the lead up to Panipat, the Marathas suffer a major setback as their veteran revenue collector Govind Pant, who was in charge of an extremely critical & strategic role, is killed in an overwhelming attack led by Atai Khan, the Durrani Wazir’s nephew.

рдХрд╛рдЮреНрдЪреА рейреи рдЬрдЧрджреНрдЧреБрд░реБ рд╢реНрд░реА-рдЪрд┐рджрд╛рдирдиреНрджрдШрдиреЗрдиреНрджреНрд░ рд╕рд░рд╕реНрд╡рддреА рдЖрд░рд╛рдзрдирд╛ #резрейрекреп

Observed on ┼Ъukla-с╣вaс╣гс╣нh─л tithi of M─Бrga┼Ы─лrс╣гaс╕е (lunar) month (Apar─Бhс╣Зaс╕е/vyaapti). The event has been commemorated since it occurred in 3773 (kali era).
Son of Kaс╣Зс╣З┼л┼Ыaс╣Еkara, the clever Padman─Бbha by ame, though intent on practising Lambika Yoga, this preceptor Cid─Бnandaghanendra adhering to the injunctions of the Master, remained in the seat of K─Бmakoс╣нi that bestows all desired things to those who resort to, fed innumerable devotees every day. He, the adept in Yoga reinstating compassionately the Kannada prince who lost kith and kin in his own kingdom through his (the princeтАЩs) conqueror, He (Cid─Бnandaghanendra) remained as preceptor only for four years sustaining on dry leaves. This preceptor reached his Ultimate abode which is devoid of all grief, delusion etc. on the sixty day of bright fortnight in the month of M─Бrga┼Ы─лrс╣гa of the year Prajotpati.

Observed on ┼Ъukla-Saptam─л tithi of M─Бrga┼Ы─лrс╣гaс╕е (lunar) month (Apar─Бhс╣Зaс╕е/vyaapti). The event has been commemorated since it occurred in 2897 (kali era).
Born of a brahmin called N─Бge┼Ыa in the village called Maс╣Еgala of the Chola country, the erudite saint well-known as ┼Ъr─л J├▒─Бnottama, foremost among logicians, having adorned the P─лс╣нha of preceptors for sixty-three years, attained salvation/siddhi on the seventh day of the bright fortnight in the month of M─Бrga┼Ы─лrс╣гa of the year Manmatha.

Observed on Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зa-Pratham─Б tithi of M─Бrga┼Ы─лrс╣гaс╕е (lunar) month (Apar─Бhс╣Зaс╕е/vyaapti). The event has been commemorated since it occurred in 3373 (kali era).
Then, the preceptor ┼Ъr─л Cidghana, having governed or held the responsibilities of ─Аc─Бrya P─лс╣нha for thirtyseven years, placed his disciple ┼Ъr─л Vidy─Бghana, who was known as ┼Ъr─л N─Бyana in P┼лrv─Б┼Ыrama before initiation, in the Maс╣нha; adhering to ascetic principles, wandering like a child, He vanished in the divine form of ─В┼Ыvara. ┼Ъr─л Sacchid─Бnanda, named ┼Ъeс╣гa (before initiation), son of ┼Ъr─лdhrapaс╣Зс╕Нita, born on the banks of river Garuс╕Нa, disciple of Preceptor Chandra┼Ыekahara having enjoyed the bliss through spiritual practices for sixty-nine years, and at the end of life entered into the ┼Ъivaliс╣ЕgaтАФK─Бy─Бdhirohane┼Ыvara. The great preceptor, the transcendental, immaculate attained the supreme state devoid of pains, beyond everything, imperishable and infinite on the first day of the dark fortnight in the month of M─Бrga┼Ы─лrс╣гa in the year Khara.
